You’ve forgotten things. I forget lots of things. And so the information by itself is actually not a very powerful way to learn. Now the second piece is activation. Now activation is a way that we assist somebody in practicing. So an example in here, I’ll be guiding you through exercises with my voice. And so because I’m guiding you through, it’s easier for you to do the exercise than if you’re trying to… to imagine it on your own. So that’s the activation part. It may go dormant, but it’s very easy to bring it back out. And I’ll give you a funny example. So I’ve got this little puppy, Lucas, and he was… Trying to get up on the daybed. I kind of showed him how he could do it and just sort of like helped him get up there one time, right? So this is the activation process. Next time he ran up, you know, he didn’t make it. Second time he made it up perfect. And then he never forgot. Once he knew that he could do it and he’d got to that place, game over. He was, you know, always on the couch from then on, which I don’t know if that was a good thing, but it’s a good example of how activation works. Even if it goes dormant, you’ll be able to bring it back very easily. Now, the third type of learning that we typically see in programs is just practice. Intro 2: How is Unlocking Transcendence different from Duality?
--------------------

Hi everybody, it’s Jeffrey and thank you so much for joining me for Unlocking Transcendence. I know you’re going to have such a great time learning about yourself and developing your higher awareness. Now, if you’re coming from the Duality program, you’ll notice there’s quite a few differences. In Duality, I really spend time going through all the descriptions and diagrams and background and models and information that you need to really get grounded in your mind so that you can experience the energy work that we’re doing in duality. And this is kind of fun because when you first start on your personal growth path or when you get into something new like energy work, your mind needs to have a lot of information so that it can relax and know that, okay, the things I’m learning make sense to me and I’m not just going off into the weeds, you know, into la -la land. And That’s why in duality, I spend a lot of time giving you that foundation for your mind. Now, by the time you’ve come to unlocking transcendence, you’re probably in a different space. And that’s why the program looks very different. So it’s natural in your personal growth to get to a space where you’re no longer really looking for information from the outside. So you’re not dependent on a teacher to tell you what to learn or you’re not dependent on books to tell you what to think. You’re actually starting to base your belief system on your own personal experiences, right? And so in Unlocking Transcendence, I lean into that part of your personal growth. So I’m not giving you a lot of background information. I’m not giving you diagrams. Basically what I’m giving you is 60 days of new experiences so that you can find your own answers. And this is really fun. The format is different as well. You’ll notice in Duality, there’s a video every day. In Unlocking Transcendence, I wanted to break this habit of depending on me, of looking for the information that you need from your teacher and getting it in the video. So you only have videos on the days where I’m giving you information, kind of at the beginning and in the integration parts of the program. The other parts, we skip that. We go directly to an audio meditation. So right away, you can go within and start to find your own answers. So that’s why we do video some days and audio the others is to break this habit of external dependency. Now, the other thing that’s really fun in Unlocking Transcendence is at the end of each day, there is a question of the day that I recommend you answer. Now, you can answer it privately for yourself if you want. And of course, it’s great if you can share it with a group. That’s fun too. But the purpose of this question is not to seek validation from the outside. What are people going to think about it? Or I got a lot of likes or comments or so on, right? So in this program, we’re turning within. The purpose of sharing is to consolidate the experience that you just had in your inner world and bring it into words. As you bring it into words, your mind will start to organize it and plug it into your belief system better. So that’s the purpose of of sharing, of answering that question of the day. Now, it’s kind of fun. The first time that we brought students through Unlocking Transcendence, I set aside my teaching hat, put on the student hat again, and I took the entire course with you for the first round. And this was really fun for me because I got to shift gears and go through as a student, do the exercises, and answer the question of the day. And so I recommend after you answer it for yourself, check out my answers for each question of the day. What you’ll find is my insights that I had each day going through, which goes a little bit deeper into each day’s teaching or each day’s investigation within. And you’ll also find out how somebody that has a fairly mature energy experience addresses questions and doubts and difficulties because things come up for me throughout the program too. So it’s kind of a nice little peek behind the scenes or, you know, kind of looking behind the curtain to see what’s really happening or the director’s cut, if you will. And I encourage you to check out that information too. You’ll find it at the bottom of the lesson. There’ll be information on how to get to each of those. So I’m really excited about this new journey for you as you start to turn within. And also when you’re posting information, you might notice that the Unlocking Transcendence group isn’t quite as interactive as the Duality group was. And that’s okay, right? Because the purpose is not the interaction with others. The purpose is self -discovery for Unlocking Transcendence. So just keep that in mind. Let’s see. The last thing I would say is the organization for Unlocking Transcendence makes it really easy. So you can’t get lost. You can’t get behind. There’s really no way to fail at this program because it’s all about your experience, your authentic experience. And I’ve organized it into six… Short quests. So there’s six 10 -day mini quests. They follow the progression that you normally go through as your awareness opens. So there’s self -awareness first, then physical awareness, mental awareness, spiritual awareness, emotional awareness, and finally impact awareness. So we go through each of those as a 10 -day quest. If you want to just do a 10 -day section at a time, that’s fantastic. But I encourage you to get to that 10 -day point before you take a break because then you’ll have that sort of completed the loop of information and experience. with that particular section. And if you want to take a few days off, check something else out, come back to it later, that’s totally fine. Again, it’s really six independent quests, although they do follow an arc or a flow throughout the whole program. Before I go, I also want to mention that the video quality is quite different between these two programs. Duality was actually shot first before unlocking Transcendence. However, it was originally shot as a live webinar series. So it was shot on web cameras and the quality was really low. So we’ve recently updated Duality with all new video and updated the content so it looks fantastic and bright and shiny and new. Unlocking Transcendence now looks a little dated by comparison because when I shot that, I filmed it myself in the place that I had rented in Sedona where I was kind of secluding myself for six weeks to really set the energy and get things just right energetically for the program. So please forgive me if the video is not quite as high quality as what you’ll see in Duality. I know you’re going to love the program anyway and really enjoy that feeling and that energy of Sedona that comes through so well in the videos. Thanks again. See you in the program.

LESSON 1: Finding Your Awareness
--------------------
Hi everybody; I'm Jeffrey Allen, and welcome to the program. I'm so glad you're here because I've got a really powerful and exciting program designed for you. And, I know that if you're here you're a spiritual seeker like me which means that you are looking for new experiences and new awareness and wanting to, you know, integrate this into your life, and really live a more fun and more spiritual life. Now, I've been teaching intuition and energy work and spiritual studies for a little over 10 years, and during that time I've taught small groups and big classes and online training. And I've taught small workshops like hour-workshops, and I've taught multiyear training programs, and it's been really fun. What's happened over that time is that, because I've been teaching and practicing, my awareness has gotten very good. It's easy for me to pick up a new awareness skill and integrate it into my daily life, and that's exactly what I want to give you in the 60 days. I want to give you that same sense that you can pick up new information easily and apply it right away in your life because I know that it's not always like that. For me, although I can do it now, it used to be very difficult. I remember when I was learning to talk to spirit guides, and I really wanted to talk to them, and I was trying everything I knew how, but for some reason it just wasn't coming; it was just out of reach. I experienced the same thing with intuition where I was trying to use my intuition to see what was happening in my environment, or, you know, apply it to my relationships, and so on. But, it just seemed just out of reach. Sometimes it worked great, sometimes it didn't work, and it was very frustrating. I'm sure you've had that same experience. And, I've seen that with my students too where some people can get the information right away, some people are excited and want it, but somehow they're not able to get the information and get the same experience. So, what I've done is looked at how can I change that. So, I listened to my students, and I watched their energy over the years, and what I noticed is that there's a base level of awareness that you need to have in several different areas for you to pick up spiritual training easily. And, I call this spiritual fitness because I think of it like, just like with physical fitness, if you wanted to run a marathon but you didn't have a certain level of fitness, you might buy some new shoes, get really excited about it, and show up on race day. Then, the gun goes off, and you start running your heart out, but you know, you're not going to make it 'cause you don't have that base level of fitness. Now, somebody else that's never run a marathon before but has a level of physical fitness, maybe they're a dancer or maybe they're a football player, but they've got this really good base level of physical fitness, they can run that marathon even the first time. It may be hard, it may be a challenge, but they can do it. And, the same thing is true in other areas of your life. If you've got your business fitness up, you can do well in business more easily. If you've got your love or relationship fitness up, you can do well in love and relationships. And, if you have your spiritual fitness up, you can do well easily in spiritual studies and spiritual growth. Now, when I talk about spiritual fitness, you actually need to be pretty flexible with your awareness to get this level of fitness up. So, there's four main types of awareness that we usually talk about. There's the body awareness, there is a mind awareness, there's emotional awareness, and then there's spiritual awareness. Those are kind of the main four categories, and each of has a different feeling to it. It has a different need and different experiences that you have in each of those. There's also, you know, before all of those, there's a basic level of just self-awareness. When you think, who am I? What happens to you? What do you, what answer do you get? And so, we're going to work on that first, self-awareness. Then, we're going to do each of these four big ones. We're going to do body awareness and spirit awareness and mind awareness and emotional awareness, not in that order. And then, we're going to do the final one which is impact awareness, which is how are you influencing other people in the world? Because it's not just about us, it's about what we're doing in the world too. Now, today we're going to start with this self-awareness, and this is really important because if you don't have a good sense of self-awareness, it can feel a little bit like you're kind of, life is happening to you, rather than feeling like you're consciously living your life and creating the things that you want. So, if you have that feeling sometimes, that life's happening to you, and I've had this too, it doesn't feel very good. Then this is what we'll start to shift in this first 10 days where we're studying self-awareness. Now, when you think about self-awareness, there's some basic questions that usually come to mind. You can ask yourself, who am I? Who, what, where, why, when, and how; those are the basic questions. And, I'm curious, for you, what do you think of those questions would be the most powerful one for developing your self-awareness? Just think about it for a minute to get it. Who, like, who am I? What am I? Where am I? When am I? How am I? Why am I here? So, what I've found over the years is that, it might kind of surprise you, but the two most powerful questions to answer to develop your self-awareness are actually, where am I? And, when am I? And, over the next 10 days, you'll understand more deeply why I say that's true. So, today we're starting with this first awareness. I just want to give you kind of a baseline understanding of, you know, who you are from the context of where. So, right now I want you to just ask yourself that question. "Where am I right now?" So, "Where am I right now?" Good, now close your eyes, and ask yourself that again. "Where am I right now?" And open your eyes again. And notice if it changed when you closed your eyes; did your awareness shift in some way? So, just right now, close your eyes, and then open your eyes. Now, sometimes people will blink a little bit as they open their eyes. What's happening there is we're kind of trained to close our eyes and then leave our body and go somewhere else. So, if your awareness got kind of weird or spaced out when you closed your eyes, that's why. Now, I want to give you a little trick that can help you get through that. So, what I want you to do now is just find a place, somewhere where your eyes rest naturally, not on the video, but somewhere in your room, and just put your eyes there, and notice your breath. And, as you're breathing, you're going to imagine you're pulling back all your awareness into this space right behind your eyes. So, just breathe, focus on that point across the room. And then, very gently on your next breath, you're going to breathe your eyes closed very slowly and see if you can maintain that same awareness right behind your eyes. Okay, good. Now, just breathe your eyes back open, and try it again. Be very focused right behind your eyes. Focus on that point. And, just breathe your eyes closed. Very good. Now, from this awareness, I want you to ask, "Where am I?" And, I want you to say out loud, "I am here." "I am here." "I am here." And, where is that here for you? Every answer's okay; just notice. Once again, just say, "I am here." And, notice any other qualities of your awareness. Is there a size that you have? Are you fuzzy? Are you clear? Are you spacey? Or, do you have a crisp awareness? Just notice; we're just having fun. Okay, so be focused behind your eyes again. And, when you're ready, just breathe your eyes open. Great, so welcome back. Now, this was a really simple exercise designed to give you that self-awareness, that kind of self-assessment of where are you naturally? We also worked on breaking one of your habits which may have been to kind of go somewhere when you close your eyes and, you know, change your focus. We're going to continue throughout the program helping you develop the habit of having that meditation awareness with your eyes open or with your eyes closed. Now, I'll share with you kind of my secret strategy here. So, there are six different steps that I take to bring your awareness from the beginning up until this base level of fitness. The first step you just did which is self assessment and breaking any old habits or establishing new habits. The second thing we'll do tomorrow which is getting an easy success. So tomorrow, you're going to actually work with your awareness inside your body, and you're going to stretch your awareness around to different places in the body. And, this will give you just an easy feeling of success, like you're doing it. The next step is to challenge you to do something a little bit more difficult, that maybe you're uncomfortable with, or you're not sure you can do, and we're going to do that the next day. So, you're going to actually move your awareness to different places inside your body, kind of like traveling around inside the body. Now, the fourth step in this strategy to do something you didn't know you could do, or something you thought wasn't even possible. So, on day four, what we're going to do is you're going to actually travel with your awareness out of your body to different places, and get an interesting experience, and then come back into your body, and this is totally safe. You know, I've done this many times; there's no problem at all. You actually leave your body every night when you sleep, so this is quite normal. And then, the fifth step, again so we did your awareness, self-assessment, and then we do you know, habits, that's step one, then we do easy success, we do a little challenge, we do kind of a wow thing where you're doing something you didn't know was possible, and then that's all the activation part. That's all what I can help you with; your base level of fitness is actually up at that point. To carry it forward, you have to practice. It's just up to you to continue your practice. Now, today, what you can do is just notice throughout the day, where are you? So, try it in different situations. Just ask yourself that question, "Where am I?" Sometime when you're feeling really happy, "Where am I?" Sometime when you're kind of frustrated and angry, "Where am I?" Or, maybe you're just feeling stuck or stressed; just ask, "Where am I?" --------------------

Hello everyone, I’m Jeffrey Allen, and welcome back to Day 2. Today you’ll be practicing focusing your awareness and stretching your awareness into different places in your body. This is important because your awareness of self is the foundation for all the exercises in this program. To begin today, I’d like you to find a place across the room where your eyes rest naturally, and focus on that point. Let your awareness be right behind your eyes, and focus on that point. Give yourself a deep breath, inhale, and exhale, maintaining your focus on this point. On your next inhale, gently close your eyes, keeping that same awareness, that same presence, behind your eyes. And ask yourself right now, where are you? Are you right behind your eyes, like in your eyelids? Are you back between your ears? Are you in the back of your head? Find your way right now to the center of your head, straight behind your eyes and right between your ears. Let your awareness be nice and focused in the center of your head. And then, without moving, I want you to notice your left ear and stretch your awareness from the center of your head. over to this ear and let your awareness return and relax to the center of your head. Again, without moving, notice your right ear and stretch your awareness from the center of your head to your right ear and relax and let it return to the center of your head. Now stretch your awareness up to the top of your head. Again, you’re stretching rather than moving and relax your awareness. into the center of your head. Now stretch your awareness down toward the top of your throat, relax to the center of your head, and stretch your awareness forward right into your eyes, and then relax to the center of your head. Stretch your awareness back to the back of your head, and then relax into the center of your head. As you did this exercise, were you able to maintain your location in the center of your head? Or did you move your awareness into the places that you were going to? For today, I want you to practice staying in the center of your head and just stretching your energy from the center of your head down to these other places. Good. Now, staying in the center of your head, stretch your awareness down toward your left shoulder and let it relax back to the center of your head. And stretch your awareness down to your right shoulder and let it relax to the center of your head. Now stretch your awareness past the left shoulder, down to the left elbow, all the way out to your left hand. Maintaining your awareness in the center of your head, stretching all the way to that left hand. And just relax. Be in the center of your head and stretch your awareness down the right shoulder. down the right arm, past the elbow, all the way into that right hand. Notice how that feels. And let your awareness come all the way back, relaxed to the center of the head. And now try both sides at once, stretching down to the shoulders, into both elbows, into both hands, and then relaxing to the center of your head. Now let’s try the next part with your eyes open. Be in the center of your head. And stretch your awareness down to your left hip, to your left knee, and into your left foot. Stretch your awareness outward to fill your entire leg, your calf and your thigh in the back. And then relax your awareness to the center of your head. Now stretch your awareness down to your right hip, your right knee, and your right foot. Remembering to stay in the center of your head. And stretch your awareness outward to fill your entire leg, your calf, your thighs, back of your leg. Notice how that feels. And then relax to the center of your head. And notice which was easier for you, working with your eyes open or with your eyes closed. And remember, it’s always okay to do whichever is more comfortable for you. So with your eyes open or closed, stretch your awareness. into your heart. Stay in the center of your head, but continue stretching your awareness into your chest, into your stomach, into your low back and your mid -back. Your upper back. Stay in the center of your head, but stretch your awareness to all points in your body at once. Notice how that feels. Notice if you’re missing any places. And then relax your awareness back to the center of your head. Have your eyes closed. Give yourself a deep breath. Let go of any effort, any bogginess or sleepiness. Smile and be amused. And when you’re ready, open your eyes. Welcome back. I hope you enjoyed your first awareness stretch. How was it for you? How did it feel? Did you like it better with your eyes open or your eyes closed? Did you find you could stretch into multiple places at once? And were you able to maintain that awareness behind your eyes in the center of your head? Or did you tend to move to the places that you were stretching to? So I’m excited to hear your answers to all those questions. So great job today. I’d like you to practice stretching your awareness today, and I’ve got three ideas that you can try on your own. First, anytime you’re stretching physically, follow up by stretching your awareness into the same areas, and just notice how much deeper your stretch feels. You can also try stretching your awareness into your hand before you’re touching somebody today, and notice how different that feels. I’d also invite you to stretch your awareness into your feet and your legs while you’re walking, and notice how much more present you are. Again, today we’re practicing staying in the center of your head, but stretching your awareness to other places in the body. So I hope that was fun, and before you go, please take one minute to share your experience in today’s exercise. LESSON 4: Travelling With Your Awareness

--------------------
Meditation: Day 4 - Traveling with your Awarenes
--------------------

Hello everyone, I’m Jeffrey Allen and welcome to day four. By now you’re noticing that although we’re doing serious spiritual work, I don’t want you to take it too seriously. When we get serious, worried, or afraid, our energy tends to slow down and get more rigid. And when we’re having fun, our energy tends to speed up and get more flexible. So having fun and being amused is the perfect state for upgrading your awareness. Today is no exception. We’re going to take a journey with your awareness today, a journey outside your body and into the stars. This is not serious business, and I definitely want you to have fun with it. If you get confused or lost or afraid, it’s always okay to open your eyes and come instantly back into your body. Or just focus on your breath with your eyes closed until you’re ready and then resume the journey with us. There is absolutely no danger of you getting stuck out of your body. In fact, you leave your body every night when you sleep, and you come back automatically when you wake up. This is quite normal, but we rarely practice it intentionally. So smile and be amused and enjoy today’s journey. As you breathe, find your awareness behind your eyes. Be relaxed, focused, and present. And gently breathe your eyes closed. LESSON 5: Location Applications & Time Awareness Intro

Hi, everyone; welcome back. I'm Jeffrey Allen, and you've made it to day five. Second day, we went through a easy success where you were able to stretch your awareness to different places in your body. Now, these first four steps are what it takes to activate your awareness. Now, the interesting thing about this is that you don't have to do it perfectly. So listening to it, going through the process, is enough to activate it even if you were falling asleep, even if you feel like you couldn't do it, even if you felt like a total failure for these first four days, you already activated that base level awareness. It shouldn't be something you have to sit down and schedule 20 minutes to do twice a day or three times a day. It should just be something that you can do all the time in your daily life because you're excited about it and you're having fun. And so I want to give you a couple of tips on how to practice your awareness in that way. Okay, so for the easy applications are just if you're not feeling present or you're feeling kind of spacey, then try that exercise where you breathe your eyes closed and stay present in the body. This is really good for getting your attention and awareness back to where it feels good. You'll notice that your productivity and your focus go way up. Now, you can use this awareness stretching that we did to really get into your body when you're waking up. I teach this to kids. I say that when you wake up, just kind of imagine you're stretching down into your body, almost like you were stretching into a sleeping bag and getting your feet all the way in and your hands all the way in. So if you're the kind of person that has a hard time waking up, try this stretching exercise with your awareness to really get into the body there. You can also use the stretching if there's some place where you have weakness or pain in the body. You can stretch your awareness into that area. And oftentimes, that's enough to kind of pop out of that stress that you're in. Now, you can also move your awareness to that place in the body and listen or have a conversation. And sometimes, this is a great way to self-diagnose or get more information about what's happening in the body. We'll actually do that in the next section when we're going into your body awareness, but you can practice it now on your own if you like. Now, if you're feeling stressed, you can also use this traveling out-of-body experience to have a little mini kind of spiritual vacation. You can go to the moon or up to the solar system or up to the edge of the universe. You can also just go to a place in your awareness that feels really peaceful and relaxing for you. You'll be surprised how much difference you can make just to get out and take a little spiritual vacation. Now, you can also use this traveling out of body if you're needing to get some more perspective. If you're feeling stuck on a particular issue, just think of the question that you're trying to solve, and then go inside, get a little bit out of your body like the corner of the room, and ask yourself the question, and then go up to the the moon and ask yourself the same question. Then, go out to the edge of the solar system and ask yourself that same question. Out to the edge of the universe; ask yourself that question. And you'll notice that you have different perspective at each of those levels. And oftentimes, this is enough to help you get through feeling like you're stuck on a particular issue. So even though these seem like really kind of funny or abstract tools, there's very specific uses that you can use in your daily life and apply these right away. Okay, so if you're wanting to do a little more advanced practice, you can start to imagine that you're stretching your awareness outside of your body, so out into your aura and so on. You can also work with your awareness to visit places you haven't been before. Maybe take a vacation to place that you want to go but you haven't been before. So that's another little stretch and you can also try out different sizes with your awareness. When you're traveling to the moon, let yourself be as big as the earth to the moon. Let yourself be as big as the whole solar system or as big as the entire universe. This is really fun to play with your awareness in this level, again, a little bit more advanced. Now, if you want to go into, you know, very advanced practice, what I'd recommend is that you play with multi-awareness. So having your awareness in more than one place at a time, and this is possible. You're doing it already. You probably just don't know you're doing it. My favorite example of this is one time when I was out four-wheeling. I had this four-wheel-drive truck. I'm coming down this trail that I probably shouldn't have been on. And at one point, I had to drive down over this big drop off, and I didn't quite have enough room. So when I did it, my truck was kind of teetering back and forth. I actually hit my front bumper on the ground rather than my tires, and I kind of panicked. I was sitting there; I felt like we were about to roll over because, you know, we were just teetering on this two tires, and I felt this little awareness, and I heard this voice over in the trees that said, "Let off the brake." And I'm used to listening to my guide, so I just let off my brake, the truck righted itself, everything was fine. And later in the day, I thought, I wonder who that was, who was helping me out. So I went into meditation, and I positioned myself on the other side of the road, of the trail, so I could see who it was. I could see myself in the truck all stressed out, panicking. Now I can see somebody appear over here and tell me, "Let off the break." Now the strange part was is that the person that appeared over there was me. It was actually me watching out for myself. And when I got that little surprise and that realization, that more aware me turned and looked directly at me and gave me a little wink. And I was really surprised. It's like, okay, I'm here watching myself, watching myself. And then, of course, I'm also meditating and watching this whole thing. So I'm in at least four different places that I'm aware of and at least two different timeframes, and this was really fun. You'll notice that as you start to play with your awareness, you'll start to have strange and amazing experiences like this too. In fact, they're happening all the time for you, but you're just not aware of it yet. And that's why this program is so important and why I want you to stick through for the whole 60 days, is that if you get your base level of fitness up in these 12 different areas, you'll start to have these experiences automatically, and it's just so fun. The next awareness that I want to help activate for you is your time awareness. And this is really important because if you're out of balance with your time awareness, it can feel pretty difficult. So for example, if you're mostly focused in the past, you can find that you'll feel very depressed, like there's no hope for the future. And sometimes, people even have a very low will to live when the energy is primarily focused in the past. If you're really focused in the future, the opposite can happen. You can feel anxious, like really nervous all the time. You can feel like you're never able to get enough or achieve enough. And if you're focused on the future, sometimes you're also not productive. You have a lot of ideas, but you're not able to make them happen. Now of course, if you're focused in the present, everything's pretty good. You're usually pretty calm. You're pretty happy. You're pretty productive. But I encourage you to develop all three of these. You want to be happy and love being with your present time awareness, with your past awareness, and with your future awareness. There's not a bad one. You just want to have balance and primarily want to be in the present moment because that's where the really powerful stuff happens. So to start developing this, we're going to do the same six steps that I recommend for developing your awareness. And the first step is a little self-assessment and changing your habits. So let's do that right now. Now, go ahead and find that point across the room, and start to breathe, and focus your energy right behind your eyes. And on your next inhale, go ahead and breathe your eyes closed. Good, now move your awareness to the center of your head, and take a little stretch. And imagine right now that there's a line beneath you that stretches out all the way to infinity on the left and all the way to infinity on the right. And one direction on this line represents the past for you and one represents your future. And your body, of course, is right in the middle in present time. From this place in present, I want you to notice how does the past line and the future line feel to you? Does one feel brighter than the other or darker than the other? Does one feel lighter or heavier than the other? Just notice. Now, focus on present time. Does present time feel light? Does present time feel bright? How does it compare to the past and the future? Now, whichever one of these is brightest for you is usually where your attention is most of the time. That's your primary focus. So just notice, are you primarily a past energy focus, present time energy focus, or future energy focus? And if you want to, I want you to imagine right now that you can balance these out. So all three of them look nice and bright, feel nice and light. Great, now forget about this timeline. Just let it fade away. Would you go to the left, or would you go to the right? Now for you, whichever direction you wanted to go naturally is likely your natural future direction. So if that's the same direction that you saw on your timeline, then your mental timeline and your experience or awareness timeline match. But if they don't, for example, if you wanted to go to the left but your mental timeline says the future is to the right, then I recommend that you flip your timeline over. So you can do, if you need to, just do that now, so that your future timeline points the direction that you wanted to walk. If it was already pointing that way, just relax and congratulate yourself. Your mental timeline and your awareness timeline were in sync. Now, feel that timeline again, stretching out to the left and to the right, and notice which one feels more comfortable for you. --------------------

Let yourself be at one moment in the future that results from this push. What’s happening in that future moment? How are you feeling? Are you happy? Move your awareness to that time and place now. Notice what happened in that time in your past. How did you feel? What did you decide about yourself or the world? Feel the momentum you created with that decision and let that momentum carry you forward through this present moment and into a new future. Notice what’s happening in that new future right now. How are you feeling? Are you happy? Is your situation better on this new future timeline? Remember the center of your head. Be here in present time. Notice the two timelines you traveled today. Will you keep this new timeline? Or do you prefer the old one? Turn toward your choice now. Breathe. Feel happy about your choice. Stretch your body. Stretch your awareness all through your body. When you’re ready, smile and open your eyes. Welcome back. Great job, everybody. I hope you had fun. Changing your future with your awareness. Now, I’d like you to practice this today. You can do it with your eyes closed or with your eyes open. Just notice several times today when your past is pushing on you and then feel that timeline that you’re on and look for a new timeline and allow yourself to turn in that new direction. And remember that you can iterate too. If you turn in a new direction, you move your awareness to the future and you don’t like that future, you can come back, pick up a third timeline, turn to that timeline, and check that one again. So I encourage you to use this at least once throughout the day today. Of course, I’d like you to share. I’d love to hear how you changed your future today. Thanks again, and I look forward to seeing you tomorrow.

LESSON 9: Time Applications & Project Timelines

--------------------

Hi everybody; I'm Jeffrey Allen, and welcome to day nine. If you don't change that momentum, it'll take you in a particular direction, but there's still a lot of probabilities out there other than that primary one that your momentum is carrying you toward. So if you start to adjust your momentum and adjust your direction, it'll take you into new directions. So I always like to say when I'm giving people intuitive readings that I don't want to always be right when I'm looking at your future, because what that means is that I'm just good at programming you to do what I said or experience what I said, and I don't want to do that. I would much rather empower you to change. If I tell you something about your future, and you don't like it, I want you to change it. I want you to change that and move into a different potential. That's the whole purpose of looking at the future is that if you don't like it, you can change it. So don't get stuck on whether you're right or wrong. Use this as an understanding of your present time future. Where am I pointed right now with my awareness? Another one that you can do is you can work with healing the body in this way. So if you, something's happening in your body, some condition that you don't like that's bothering you and you want to change, you can travel with your awareness back in time to a place where you didn't have that problem. And once you have those two end points, you kind of come back toward the middle into present time. So you're kind of working both ends of the time and bringing it back to you. LESSON 27: Hearing Your Personal Filter

--------------------
Meditation: Day 27 - Hearing Your Personal Filter
--------------------

Hello everyone, I’m Jeffrey Allen. Welcome to day 27 of your mind awareness challenge. This is your challenge day for your outer mind awareness. And what I want you to get today is a sense of your own filters, your opinions and your perceptions, and I want you to begin to see through them. This is really great for breaking through any mental ceiling that you have because it’s going to help you see things in a new way. It’s also great for communicating with other people and developing more compassion in your mind. So let’s dive in. Focus on a point across the room where your eyes rest naturally, and have your awareness right behind your eyes. Notice your breath, and when you’re ready, breathe your eyes closed, maintaining that same awareness behind your eyes. And take a moment to get really present in your body. Stretch your awareness into your hands and your feet and all through your body. Think of something that you have a strong opinion about right now. Might be politics or sports, personal health or something else. And just notice your opinion about that issue. And in your mind’s eye, see yourself telling your story about this issue right now. Listen to your story as you tell all the details. And what’s your favorite part? What do you really like to say about this topic? Hear yourself saying those words, the same ones you’ve said before, and notice how fun it is to share your opinion with others. Notice all the people who agree with you, and all those people that you might convince, and notice how absolutely compelling and true your story feels right now. Good. Now, begin to notice Who else have you heard tell this story? Is this your original story? Or did it start with somebody else? And notice any similar stories that you’ve told in the past. Is this story new? Or is it a rerun or remake of an older story? And notice any pain or frustration that you’re holding around this issue. And start to let that go right now. You don’t need to carry this pain or frustration anymore. Just breathe and let it go. Now ask yourself, is this really a true story? Have you enhanced it or embellished it to make your case? Are you leaving out some information that doesn’t help your case? Just be amused and enjoy your creativity. Now let that story go and think about the opposite story. Somebody that has the opposing opinion, a completely different story that you tend to disagree with or maybe ignore. And let yourself be an amusement and temporarily adopt this story as your own. And try to do it authentically without sarcasm or judgment. And hear yourself telling the story with the same enthusiasm as before. Now this is your stretch, so really let yourself get into character. As you tell those details of this opposing opinion, just imagine that you’re completely convinced that they’re true. Think about all the people who agree with you. Think of all the people you might convince. And notice how it feels to tell this story with enthusiasm and commitment. Does it feel the same or different than before? Be amused. Now take a neutral position. Be an observer watching both sides of these stories. Be aware, but completely detached from the outcome. Now remember your honest opinion and see yourself expressing that side of the story right now with passion and commitment. And really admire your enthusiasm and your dedication. And notice how bright you shine. And from this neutral position, see someone else telling the opposing side of the story, with that same passion and commitment, and really admire their enthusiasm and their dedication. Notice how they shine. And from this place of neutrality, notice the similarities between the characters and the stories. While the details differ, the themes are likely the same. There might be a good guy and a bad guy. Maybe a scary outcome or a miraculous outcome. Notice where they’re the same. Now let the details of these stories fade away and focus on the people. Notice their passion, their desire to make the right choice, and their desire to help others. have compassion for their pain and their frustration, and admire these very similar people with very different stories. Send love and appreciation to both people and both sides of the story. And notice it doesn’t matter which story you hear. They’re both stories. Notice your body again. Be in that room in the center of your head. And begin to notice all the stories here. that you’re holding onto as truth. Shine that blue light around and clear any mental fog that’s hiding pain or frustration around those stories. And let any pain or frustration fade away into that light. As it clears, let go of any stories or opinions that you no longer need. Everything that’s not serving you. Everything that’s just noise. Move it out of this room right now. Breathe. Admire how much more freedom you have right now. Smile. And open your eyes. Welcome back. Great job. Today was a challenge day, so it’s okay if this exercise was difficult or even frustrating. That’s by design. That’s how we grow. So I hope you were able to find that neutral position and see the people behind the stories. Because when you can do this in life, Even the deepest arguments can be really graceful or beautiful to perceive. To gain a little more practice at this today, I want you to listen to one conversation, one person that you disagree with, as if everything they were saying is true. And just notice how much fun that they’re having, even if you don’t agree. Don’t interrupt them or rewrite or edit. Just enjoy the show. Try responding to the person instead of responding to their story. Maybe you say, wow, I can really feel your enthusiasm and commitment to that opinion. That’s great. And if you’re telling your own opinion, your own stories, try starting them with something like, in my opinion, or I heard someone say, and let them be stories instead of needing to pretend that they’re absolutely true. One more quick tip. The goal here is not to get rid of your opinions, but just to be aware of them and aware that they’re stories and that they may change over time. So I’d love to hear how this experience was for you today, just what surprised you about today’s challenge, and could you see the beauty of the people beneath those opposing stories? Thanks so much for today, and I will see you tomorrow.

And even more what happened was that, if I hadn't sold that house within the next few months, I probably would've been in trouble because about two months after I sold, the US housing market started to crash, and it just went down, down, down, and I probably would've lost that house and the money that I had into it. So in that case, listening to the flow and going with the flow was much better than what I had planned. So kind of a fun story. Another way to practice this awareness is if you're in a meeting or a conversation and people are having a difficult time getting along, if you notice two really distinct opinions that seem that they're opposing, if you listen a little bit deeper with your awareness, oftentimes you'll notice that beneath that there is a common goal and there is common ground. LESSON 41: Welcome to Emotion Awareness
--------------------

Hi everybody; I'm Jeffrey Allen, and welcome to day one of your Emotion Awareness Challenge. Now emotional awareness is one of my favorite awarenesses to look at, and I saved it till the end here because it tends to be a little bit more unconscious than the other types of awareness because we we like to hide our emotions. But I know that now you've got your awareness up pretty good. You've been practicing your tools, and you can handle it now and really get in and see the emotions in a really good way. Now, I've been practicing helping people with their emotions and kind of understanding them and unwinding them and finding out what's happening there for about 10 years in private sessions. And this is super fun because it's kind of like being a little sleuth, where you're looking inside and finding out what is this emotion? And where did it come from? How do you let it go? It's actually very fun to work with emotions; it's kind of a surprise. And this is what I want to share with you in this training, is get you to that same place where, for other people's emotions and your own emotions, you've just got a curiosity and enthusiasm and excitement about working with emotions instead of kind of, you know, not wanting to deal with them. Now, it's pretty easy for me to tune into emotions and work with people and express my own emotions and so on, but it wasn't always that way. So my background is really more from the mental side of the game. I was very mental in college, and the mind was kind of the important thing, and emotions were just something that, like, I kind of didn't understand, didn't really value that much. And it was pretty frustrating because I actually had a very high emotional sensitivity, but I had a very low emotional awareness. And so, this led to me feeling like it was pretty hard to communicate, and I really didn't know how I was feeling most of the time. Basically, I just kind of was either happy or I was grumpy and didn't understand. And this might sound familiar to some of you, and what happened over the years, was that I started to notice that emotions are different than what I thought, that emotions are playing all the time. So, all of your emotions are playing inside you all the time and around you all the time. It's a bit like a radio station; if you think about how the radio works, all the radio stations are playing all at the same time, but you don't hear them all because you've just got the dial set to a particular station. And your emotions are like this, they're all playing all the time. You have all the emotions inside you, and your station tuner will go to one or the next, and that's when it'll kind of come up, and you'll feel the emotion. And with practice, you can learn how to tune that dial where you want it to be. And this is really fantastic because as the emotional awareness goes up, it feels like you're a lot more level and that you're kind of more in control of your emotions. And I say that because when you don't have emotional awareness, it definitely feels like things are out of control; they just kind of happen. Most of us have a default emotional state that kind of gets triggered at times. And for me, mine was anger, and people laugh when I tell them this now 'cause I'm not an angry person. But before, I had this anger inside me; I didn't even know it was there, but it was there all the time. It was just something that had happened when I was a kid, that I was angry about, and never let go. And this anger was the default emotion. So, if something was surprising, boom, I got angry. If, you know, pretty much anything that happened, if it was out of my control, anger would come up in me, whether expressed or not. Like I said, I didn't even know this was happening. And what I did to clear this over the years, and kind of get out of that space, was I learned some really important emotional tools. I learned one, that it's much better to be honest and aware of your emotions than to kind of stuff 'em and hide 'em, right? And to do that, you have to get out of judgment. You have to stop thinking of your emotions and yourself as something bad or someone bad when you're having your emotions. And then, of course, you need to clear your unconscious triggers. So, whatever's kind of popping those, making them come up, if you can clear those, you'll feel a lot better. And then starting to view your emotions as just signposts along the way. So they're helping you understand where you are, so you can make a choice, and move to somewhere different if you choose. So they're not destinations that you have to hang out at; they're just signposts along the way. Now, the way that I got myself kind of out of this stuck place, out of this low awareness, was I took a two-year training class with The ManKind Project. It's actually just a weekend training, and then I studied with a group of men. Every week, for several hours, we'd get together and just dive in really deep to emotional work. And we were together for two years, and over that time, just amazing emotional progress happened. After a year in there, these guys were... I mean, we're really close; we're talking about everything. We totally trust each other. And it took me a year before I realized that I wasn't being honest, not with them, I wasn't being honest with myself, and so I couldn't be honest with them. It was a big breakthrough. And then, about a year later, I was getting pretty good at like, "Oh, what am I actually feeling?" "How do I express it?" "How do I let go of any judgments about it?" And then of course, in the last 10 years, I've worked with a lot of people who have similar emotional things or working on getting their emotional awareness up. And it's fantastic. And I'm really excited about this particular part for you. We're going to work in two different sections for your emotions. The first awareness is going to be just in the feeling part. "So how do you feel your emotions?" And we'll start with that today. The second part is about empathy which is actually feeling other people's emotions or connecting with the energy that's around you. And I'll talk about that in more detail when we get there. So, let's go ahead and get started on the feeling part. Today we're going to do that self-assessment. Tomorrow we're going to go into an easy exercise where we can just feel all those emotions inside you. The Challenge Day, we're going to go in and look at "How do you find that default emotion for you?" Mine was anger, but how do you find yours? And then clear it and start to get rid of that, so you don't have that, you know, kind of burst of anger, sadness, or fear, whatever comes up as the default for you. And then, of course, on the Wow Day we're going to just go to build a little map where all your emotions actually lead to gratitude and joy if you know how to do that. So that'll be the Wow Day. So, let's dive in for today and do your self-assessment. Go ahead and close your eyes. Let your awareness be right behind your eyes and in the center of your head. Smile and be amused. Do you judge your emotional self? Are you enemies? Let's check the basic five emotions for you, and just notice do they feel like they're positive or negative or neutral for you? And use a little gauge; positive, negative, and neutral. So, first check happiness. Is this a positive emotion, Negative emotion, or neutral? How about sadness? Is this positive? Or negative? Or neutral? What about anger? Do you see it as positive, or negative, or neutral? And fear? Is it positive, negative, or neutral for you? What about shame? Positive, negative, or neutral? Ask yourself, "How are your emotions affecting your satisfaction with your life?" Is it positive, they're adding to it? Negative, where they're taking away from your satisfaction? Or just neutral? Ask yourself, "How are your emotions affecting your personal relationships?" Are your emotions having a positive effect on your relationships? A negative effect? Or neutral? LESSON 45: Emotion Applications + Intro To Empathy

Hi everyone; I'm Jeffrey Allen, and welcome to day five of your Emotion Awareness Challenge. Today you're finishing your activation for your emotional feeling awareness. So congratulations. To do this, we went through those six steps to awareness success. First step was getting more awareness to self-assessing how do you feel about your emotions and which one is your default emotion? And the next day we did the Easy Day where you kind of looked at feeling all of your emotions, just giving yourself permission to really feel them and have them. And I hope it was easy; might have been challenging. And the next day we did the challenging exercise where we looked at that default emotion that kind of pops up and took you in to find that emotion and to heal that and bring it out so it can start to finally clear out of your space. Really powerful exercise; you'll notice that'll just kind of keep going and going; you'll heal more and more from that default emotion. Then yesterday on the Wow Day, we looked at building a map. So whatever emotional state you're in, you can use that blue light and kind of find your way to the next step and the next step and the next step, until eventually you can get all the way back to gratitude and joy. Now keep in mind, sometimes that'll take more than just 10 minutes; sometimes if it's really deep, it may take you a couple days. But if you follow that approach, it's a great way to build and to use your emotional awareness. Now the fifth step and sixth step are just practicing and sharing. And of course, you know, those are up to you. I wrote down some exercises, some applications that you can use to use this awareness and to practice it more, so let's take a look. Okay, first for your personal life, just noticing your emotions, making friends with them, not hiding them, you'll notice that you are going to feel so much better. And seeing them as those signposts that lead to gratitude and joy is a big part of that acceptance and kind of relief; it's okay to have them. If you do find yourself stuck in a particular emotion a lot, think about redrawing a map from that emotion for you all the way into gratitude and joy because you may need a specific map that works just for you and just for your situation. For your relationships, if you can work with just practice not becoming your emotions. And by that, I mean when an emotion comes up, you can feel it, but you don't kind of blow up and become the emotion. And this will also help you talk a little bit more about your emotions with, when you can feel 'em and not become 'em, they're more of a curiosity and you can start to say things like, "Ah, I'm feeling sadness. I wonder why." Or, "I'm starting to feel some anger; I wonder what's going on with me." Because you haven't become them, so you're able to still have a conversation, and you'll find that this is really fun in a partnership because then you get to have a dialogue about it instead of just, you know, blowing up. Much better. And if you're feeling emotionally overwhelmed in your relationship, use that same blue light exercise where you're seeing that blue light and going toward relief to where you feel step-by-step just a little bit better until you can move into gratitude and joy. In your work and money and career space, you'll notice that your high emotions are not always welcome at work. And so if you notice your emotions are getting really high, I encourage you to hold off from doing things like sending emails or making big decisions because you really want to let those emotions pass first because sometimes what feels great when you're emotionally charged isn't the best thing for your career or your friendships. So I encourage you, just be aware of your emotions before you're firing off emails and making decisions. Now, a little more advanced work you can do is go into that emotional room, use that blue light and that divine gold light to clear the unconsciousness and to heal your emotions. You could even organize and explore them a little bit more and just work on, you know, coming from curiosity and nonjudgment, and you'll realize that this is really, really fun. Now, today, we want to move into your next awareness which is your emotional empathic awareness. And your empathy is really a simple word for saying that emotions are contagious. So if people around you are feeling happy, you tend to feel happy. If people around you are feeling grumpy, you tend to feel grumpy. Now, different people have different levels of emotional sensitivity or different levels of empathy. And this doesn't mean that they're aware; this just means that they're sensitive, right? And so for me, for example, I was always very sensitive empathically, but like I mentioned before, I wasn't really that aware of my emotions, so I would tend to, you know kind of match people and not even realize that it wasn't my emotion I was feeling. So if somebody else was upset, I would just be feeling upset and grumpy. I thought it was mine. And people do this all the time, I see this so much in my private sessions, when you start getting this clarity about which of your emotions are actually yours and which emotions belong to other people and you're just feeling, you notice that, wow, all of a sudden some of the big emotional challenges you thought you had aren't even yours, and you don't have to process them or deal with them. You can just let 'em go. And we'll go into that in more detail later. Now it sounds like the empathy, 'cause it's just kind of a problem, you know, like lose yourself, feel other people's emotions, but it's actually a very good social skill too. So people that are highly empathic can fit in really well into social environment. You can also cheer up really easily if you're highly empathic. And if you get it under control so that you are broadcasting what you want, you can actually influence people very effectively with your empathy. And one more kind of fun thing with empathy is that if you're empathically sensitive you tend to enjoy movies more, right? So is there anybody that cries at a sad movie? Yeah, that's me. You know, because you can really feel the emotions, and this is fun because all the emotions are fun. That's why we go to scary movies and we go to like, you know, shoot 'em ups, and we go to sad movies, is that all the emotions are fun and we enjoy feeling them. It's just part of the spice of life. So again, if these are out of balance in you, if your empathy is out of balance, you're going to feel kind of like an emotional sponge, you might feel wishy-washy where you're changing your mind, or get overwhelmed a lot, or be kind of like volatile. And that was me, I was kind of volatile. And if they're just right, the opposite will happen, you'll feel like tuned in to other people, but more importantly, other people will think that like you really get them. When you're around somebody they'll think, "Wow, he or she really gets me and understands me and has compassion for me and has a connection to me." And so if you're a healer or a counselor or work with people in any way, having empathy awareness is fantastic because it allows you to connect, you know; it's a great social skill. Okay, one more thing that's kind of funny is I noticed when I moved to Japan, that there seems to be a big cultural bias with our empathy as well. So in Japan, there was a woman who was working with a friend of mine in the U.S. And at one point, she got really frustrated and said, "I'm just so angry at him because he always thinks about himself first." And I know a little bit about Japanese culture; you know, my wife is Japanese, and I told her, "Well, actually, I don't think you understand American culture; we don't and think about ourselves first, we just think only about ourselves. In fact, that's what we're trained to do: take care of number one." And I said, "But in Japan, they're actually trained from the time they're very young to always think about everybody else first. How will your actions influence somebody else? You always think about the other people before yourself." And I told her, "You know neither one of these is really good or bad; neither of them are actually very balanced. So what you want to do is you want to think about yourself and other people at the same time. You know, you're just kind of equals. Is it good for me? Is it good for everybody else? You don't have to put yourself first, like we learn to do in America, and you don't have to put yourself last like people learn to do in Japan." So just kind of a little fun insight on empathic awareness I wanted to share. Okay, so today we're going to get started with just a self-assessment as we always do. So just relax and get ready. And when you're ready, you can close your eyes. And be present right behind your eyes. And as you breathe, really feel your body present in your body and be relaxed. And think about how sensitive you are, how empathic, or how stable are you with your emotions? Imagine you're feeling really good. And you walk into a room full of grumpy people. Does your mood usually change or do you stay happy? Now what about if you're at work and there's a little noise or you're trying to focus; maybe people are laughing. Is it easy for you to block that out? Or is it completely distracting for you? Now think about your preferences. Do you have strong preferences or weak preferences or kind of suppressed preferences? So for example, if you're going out to dinner with a few friends, and somebody asks, "What would you like for dinner?" How do you respond? Do you tell 'em exactly what you want for dinner? Do you have a strong preference? Or do you say, "I'll just go where everybody else wants to go." You have a weak preference. Or do you go along with the flow, but then get a little angry or have some kind of suppressed resentment or anger about it? The last two are high emotional sensitivity or high empathic sensitivity. And now think about making a decision like a recent decision you had to make. Did you just make the decision quickly based on what works for you? That's a low empathic awareness. Or did you move really slowly and consider all the angles? How's it going to affect everybody? Maybe go back and forth a few times with the decision. This is more of a high empathic awareness. And just notice what are you feeling now? And see if you can notice who you are feeling right now. In fact, put up a little gauge and ask yourself, "From 0 to 100%, what percentage of my emotions that I'm feeling now are mine? And what percentage of my emotions that I'm feeling now are somebody else's?" Just be amused. And let's create a little gauge that we're going to use later on, a simple gauge for deciding is something mine or not mine? You just see that gauge in front of you and test it out by saying your name out loud. Whichever way the gauge went, that's the side that's yours. And then say somebody else's name. Gauge is showing you, ah, that's not yours. Now let's spice this gauge up a little bit. So if you like visuals, add a little color. As you say your name, what color do you get? As you say somebody else's name, what different color do you get? Now add a little bit of sound in there. As you say your name, what do you hear and your tone? And as you say somebody else's name, notice what you hear, a different tone. Add a little feeling and emotion to this gauge, so when you say your name, how does it feel? And when you say somebody else's name, how does that feel? Pick one emotion that you're feeling right now; try out this new gauge. Just ask yourself, "For this emotion, is it mine or is it not mine?" Good, and just be amused, whatever answer you got. Give yourself a deep breath. And when you're ready open your eyes. All right. Welcome back; good job. And whatever answer you got, keep in mind that high or low sensitivity with your empathy is not a good or a bad thing; you just want to know what it is for you. So if you're a person that has strong preferences and you know where you want to go, you make decisions quickly, usually you think of this as a strong person. And you actually are strong in your preference but you have a low empathic sensitivity, and this is probably perfect for you. Now, if you're the other way where you're wishy-washy or you're following the crowd or, you know, you don't have strong preferences, this is totally okay too. This just means that you have a different personality, and you have a high sensitivity with your empathy. Now, either way, we're going to work over the next couple days and help you get a little more practice working with and understanding empathy and especially this idea of what's yours and what's not yours. So if you want to practice this today, use that gauge today as you walk around and just notice a few things that you're feeling, and ask, "Is it mine or not mine?" Okay, great. So please share what that experience was like for you. I'd love to hear, like, what is that gauge like for you? And also, if you have any experiences about empathy that are positive, please share that too. Thanks so much for today, and I will see you tomorrow.

LESSON 46: Being Consciously Empathic

--------------------
Meditation: Day 46 - Being Consciously Empathic
--------------------

Hello everyone, I’m Jeffrey Allen. Welcome to day six of your Emotion Awareness Challenge. This is your easy success day for your empathy awareness. And what I want you to get today is just a sense that you can easily change the channel on your empathy and your emotions, and that you can use your empathy to tune into the emotions that you want to. And this is really great for changing your emotional state consciously and building up that emotional confidence that you really have control or that you’re not out of control with your emotions. Okay, so let’s begin. Find a point across the room where your eyes rest naturally. Focus on that point and breathe your eyes closed. Have that same awareness behind your eyes as you move into the center of your head. Admire this space, this room in the center of your head, and make your way into the room of your emotions right now. Remember, this is a safe place to explore your emotions with curiosity and clarity. Think about your favorite comedian, your funniest person you know, or some joke that you love. And notice how you feel. As you think about this person, notice how much fun they’re having and start to match their energy. As you do, notice how you become funnier too. And notice, do you have any friends who make you funnier? It’s because you’re matching their energy. Now remember a favorite scene in a movie where one of the characters is having some deep emotions. Notice what they’re feeling. It might be sadness or fear or anger or joy. Can you feel those emotions with them? Now think of a speaker that you really admire, somebody giving a really inspiring speech. Can you feel the strength of their emotions? How does this help you align behind their cause? Now imagine you’re in your life now. Imagine you’re working in an office where you interact with other people. And you’re in some public space in this office and you’re feeling really positive. Really feel that positive energy, that positive mood right now. Next, someone feeling negative walks into the space. They’re grumpy and complaining. By the time they leave, you’re feeling grumpy and negative too. Feel that energy. Congratulations, you’ve matched their energy and their mood. Be amused. Next, imagine someone feeling positive walks in. They’re bright and they’re happy, laughing and smiling. Feel yourself beginning to cheer up. And remember your positive mood. Congratulations, you’ve matched their energy and mood. Just be amused. Now rewind the scene and be aware of your empathy, your ability to match other people’s energy and emotions. Remember you’re in the space, you’re feeling really positive, and someone feeling negative walks into the room. Empathically, you feel what they feel. You notice they are feeling negative. And you’re aware, but you don’t become their emotions. Just hold on to your positive emotional state. And now say something to validate yourself and to validate them. Something like, sounds like you’re grumpy. I’m actually feeling really good today. Just acknowledge and be aware of their emotions without matching their emotions. Notice how that feels. Now imagine the positive person walks in. Notice their positive energy, but keep your own positive energy. Say something like, you look really positive today. I’m feeling great too. And notice that you can be independently happy. Notice that your emotions are your responsibility. It’s not the grumpy person’s fault that you matched their energy. That’s your responsibility. That’s your fault. If you take responsibility, this will stop happening. Say out loud now, my emotions are my responsibility. Smile and be grateful. One more time. My emotions are my responsibility. Great. Now let’s really put this to the test. Imagine now you get called into a private meeting with somebody that’s grumpy about you. Maybe they didn’t like something you did and they’re not being very nice about it. As you experience this, remember, my emotions are my responsibility. Their emotions are their responsibility. Notice their emotions, but keep your happiness. And while this person’s being grumpy to you, notice the phone rings and it’s their spouse. When they answer, they’re suddenly happy and cheerful and kind to their spouse. Just notice their emotions and be amused. And when they hang up and say, ah, where was I? And then they get grumpy again. Just watch and be amused. Their emotions have nothing to do with you. As they get wound up again, validate their positive emotions. Say something like, it sounds like you really enjoy your spouse. And smile. Notice what happens. As you leave their office, Keep your feeling of happiness. Your emotions are your responsibility. Be in the center of your head, stretch into your body, give yourself a deep breath, and open your eyes. Welcome back. Great job. I hope you got a sense that you are empathic and that you do match people, but that you can choose to change the channels. And in the next few days, we’ll be refining exactly that skill. Now, to deepen this awareness today, try matching somebody consciously today just to gain an understanding and awareness of them and also to notice that you can do this consciously. This is actually a great social skill. And if someone negative comes up today, practice this exercise. Say something like, it looks like you’re feeling grumpy or bad or down, but I’m feeling pretty good. And just see how that changes their mood. And today I’d like you to share if you are able to keep your own emotions around other people or if you’re very easily swayed. I’m just curious for you, what’s your experience with that? Thank you so much for today and I will see you tomorrow.
