LESSON 47: Clearing Empathic Emotions

--------------------
Meditation: Day 47 - Clearing Empathic Emotion
--------------------

Hello everyone, I’m Jeffrey Allen. Welcome to day seven of your Emotion Awareness Challenge. This is your challenge day for your empathy awareness. And today I want you to do some emotional, empathic housecleaning. We’re going to clear out any stored emotions that you’ve matched from other people in the past. And this is really great for just finding your authentic self and for getting off any weird emotional roller coasters that you may have been riding. So you’re going to find this to be really powerful. Now, a couple tips today. There’s two main methods for processing your emotions. The first one is pretty well known, and that’s if something is really yours and your emotion, you want to own it, take responsibility for it, process it, heal it, mend it, and so on. This is pretty common. But this is only appropriate for emotions which are yours. For emotions which are not yours, the appropriate action is to disown them, to not take responsibility for these emotions, but to take responsibility for putting them in your space and responsibility for letting them go. Now, this is not a cop-out. This is actually an appropriate response to emotions that are not yours. You just want to move them out of your space. I was in a sweat with a Native American group, and they had a really nice saying for this. They were just praying to this great spirit, and they said, please take this and put it somewhere where it won’t hurt anyone anymore. And I love that because it’s a graceful way of releasing a negative energy. Okay, let’s begin. Find a point across the room where your eyes rest naturally. Focus on that point. And breathe your eyes closed. Let your awareness move into that room in the center of your head. Admire this room. Find that door to your emotional room. And make your way into this emotional room. This safe place for you to explore your emotions. And then let yourself have that blue light in one of your hands. Begin clearing any unconscious energy, any emotional fog. And in the other hand, hold that divine golden light, which is for healing. And imagine there’s a simple gauge out in front of you that can tell you if something is mine or not mine. And you can test this gauge. Just say your name. And that is your mind setting. And say somebody else’s name. Okay, now that’s not mine. Let’s have a little more fun with this gauge today. If you like visuals, add some color to it. What color means mine? What color is not mine? If you like sounds, add a tone. What sound is mine? What sound is not mine? If you like feelings, add a feeling to this gauge. What feeling is mine? What feeling is not mine? All right, great. In this emotional room, notice all the energy of happiness and ask this gauge to show you all the happiness that is yours. Begin to own all that happiness, take responsibility for it, surround it with that gold healing light, and love all that happiness that is truly yours. Now let that gauge show you all the happiness which is not mine. For this happiness, let it go. Take responsibility for bringing it in and responsibility for letting it go. Put a blue light around that happiness that’s not yours and see it loosen up and float away. And now be aware of all this sadness in this emotional room. And use your gauge to separate it into two parts. All the sadness that’s yours and the sadness that’s not yours. And for all the sadness that is yours, own it right now. Take 100 % responsibility for all the sadness that’s yours and surround it with that gold healing light and really love this sadness. And for the sadness that’s not yours, I want you to disown it. Only take responsibility for letting it go. See that blue light surrounding it and beginning to loosen it. And let that sadness that’s not yours float away to somewhere where it won’t hurt anyone anymore. Breathe. Now be aware of all the anger in this emotional room. Use your gauge again to separate it into two groups. The anger that’s truly yours and the anger that belongs to someone else. And for the anger that’s yours, really own it right now. Take 100 % responsibility for this anger that’s yours and surround it with the golden healing light and really love this anger. Good. Now, for the anger that’s not yours, I want you to disown it right now. Only take responsibility for letting this anger go. See that blue light surrounding all the anger that’s not yours. Let it loosen up and float away to somewhere where it won’t hurt anyone anymore. Good. Now, become aware of all the fear in this room of your emotions. Use your gauge to notice what fear is truly yours. And what fear belongs to someone else? For the fear that’s yours, really own it. Take total responsibility for that fear and begin to surround it with that golden healing light. Love this fear. And for the fear that’s not yours, disown it. Only take responsibility for letting it go. Surround that fear that’s not yours with a blue light. Just let it loosen. And float away to somewhere where it won’t hurt anyone anymore. Now notice all the emotion of shame in this room. And let your gauge tell you the part that’s your shame and the part that’s somebody else’s shame. And just be curious, be amused. And for the shame that’s yours, really own it. Take 100 % responsibility for that shame and surround it with gold healing light. And really love this shame. And for the shame that’s not yours, disown it now. Only take responsibility for letting it go. See that blue light surrounding it and loosening it. And let all that shame that’s not yours float away to somewhere where it won’t hurt anyone anymore. Now be aware of any other energy in the room you haven’t worked with so far. Use the gauge to notice all the energy that’s yours and any remaining energy that’s not yours in this emotional room. And for the energy that’s not yours, disown it right now. Only take responsibility for letting it go. See that blue light surrounding any other emotional energy that’s not yours? Let that energy loosen and simply float away to somewhere where it won’t hurt anyone anymore. Now take 100 % responsibility for all the energy in this room. Surround it all with gold healing light, and love all the energy in your emotional room. Take 100 % responsibility for your emotions, for keeping this room clean, and for loving your emotions. Now move your awareness up into that main room in the center of your head and take a step into your workroom. Use this gauge in here and notice all the energy in your workroom that’s yours and all the energy that’s not yours. For all the energy that’s yours, take 100 % responsibility for it. Surround it with this gold healing light. Love it. For all the energy that’s not yours in your workroom, disown it. Only take responsibility for letting it go. See that blue light surrounding it and loosening it. Let all the energy that’s not yours just float away. And take a step into your planning room where you make your plans. Again, use your gauge. Notice all the energy in your planning room that’s yours and all the energy that’s not yours. And for the energy that’s not yours, disown that energy. Only take responsibility for letting it go. Let that blue light surround it, loosen it up, and see all the energy in your planning room that’s not yours float away. And for the energy that’s yours, take 100 % responsibility for it. If you want to deepen this practice today, just practice a few times as you walk around what’s mine and what’s not mine. You can use this gauge for anything. It’s fantastic. And then please share. Hi everyone; I'm Jeffrey Allen, and welcome to day nine of your Emotion Awareness Challenge. And congratulations, you've completed your activation for your empathy awareness. And we did that by going through those six steps to awareness success, did a self-assessment of how sensitive you are to other people's energy and how empathic you are. So really good empathic awareness. So I'm going to give you some exercises, some examples of how to practice. Let's take a look. Now, of course, the easiest application is just using that ability to notice what's yours and what's not yours. So one, first, what are you actually feeling? And then is it yours or is it not yours? So that's just a kind of a basic application. Now this works in your body and with your health too. So oftentimes if you start developing this awareness, you'll notice that some of the pain that you have in your body is not actually your pain. That sounds kind of strange, but it's true. If you notice that your knee is a little funny or your back is a little funny, ask yourself, "Whose pain is this?" And if it's not yours, just move it out. Disassociate from that pain. And most times it'll just go away. It's actually a really powerful tool to work with your body. Now in relationships, you'll find that if you can hold your own space, not become your partner's emotions, that you'll have a lot deeper compassion and that you'll actually be able to be present for them so they can talk about their emotions and practice and move through it and heal it and so on without becoming their emotions and kind of joining their cause and getting angry or frustrated or sad with them. It's actually much nicer to have a partner who can empathize with your emotions or sympathize with them but not empathize or become the emotions that you're having. So this is really great. Now with work this happens too because you want to be able to choose your emotions at work and be more even keel than you would maybe in a personal relationship. And you'll notice that if you can do this, if you can handle your emotions well, people will really start to trust you. And they'll, they'll listen to you more, and you'll have more credibility because they know that you're not just kind of, you know, popping from your emotions, that you're actually a stable, emotional person. So it's really great. Some advanced applications are that if you notice that you are matching somebody, say you're matching their anger or their pain, like somebody yells at you and blows up and you just start to get angry too. So try not to fight back with that person, even though the energy's coming up and your emotion's coming up just notice, "Okay, I've got a deeper awareness I'm going to practice right now." Take a few deep breaths and just think about not spreading that to the next person because, if one person gets angry and then you catch it and you get angry and the next person and so on, this is how these negative emotions and challenging emotions move all around the planet. If one person can stop it and just say, and you can be that person, and say, "All right, I'm feeling angry or feeling sad. I'm just going to take a few breaths. I'm going to work on it before I pass it on to the next person." And what happens there is you break that chain, and you'll start noticing that your relationships are much, much better, and you just feel better about yourself 'cause you're not passing that along. Okay, I want to do just one more fun exercise with you today. One kind of new application where you can use your empathy to tune in to a group of people. So say if you're going to a party or a conference or somewhere, and there's people that you don't know very well, you can actually use your empathy to tune in and find the people that you want to connect with and then have a better conversation with those people. So let's do a little meditation and let's practice that right now. Go ahead and close your eyes. Be present right behind your eyes. And really feel your body; feel yourself being in your body and aware. Now imagine that you are about to walk into a party or a conference. You're outside the door. You're by yourself, and you don't know many people inside. Notice how you're feeling right now, and use that blue light to show you a way step by step to move into gratitude and joy. Maybe it's as simple as just being grateful that you're at this event and just a joy to be alive. And with that feeling, enter the room, and just be happy and curious what you'll find. Use your empathy awareness to feel the room. Is it mostly happy or is it nervous or serious? Does it feel like fun? And don't match the energy; just notice the energy. Now begin to scan the room with your empathy, or use that blue light to guide you either way. Feel around until you find an emotion that feels good to you. Where is it in the room? And then begin walking toward that place. As you walk, notice someone with kind of a ruffled energy that's approaching you. And try to avoid them, but they accidentally bump into you. What happens with your emotions? Did you snap into a default emotion? Maybe anger or surprise; fear? If so, just be amused, and let that emotion fade. Return to feeling happy and curious, and start walking again toward that place that feels good to you. As you walk through different areas in the room, notice how people are feeling. Use your empathy notice the emotions, but don't match them. Don't become other people's feelings. Notice how easy this is. Smile and enjoy your awareness.
